// Server.js - Version 39.13 - Hanterar multi-fr√•gor genom att dela upp dem
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const MiniSearch = require('minisearch');
// --- IMPORTER F√ñR OPENAI ---
require('dotenv').config();
const { OpenAI } = require('openai');
const openai = new OpenAI();
// ----------------------------

const app = express();
const PORT = 3000;
const KNOWLEDGE_DIR = path.join(__dirname, 'knowledge');

app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());
// --- GLOBALA VARIABLER ---
let miniSearch;
let allChunks = [];
let knownCities = [];
const levenshteinCache = new Map();
const CACHE_LIMIT = 1000;

// --- HJ√ÑLPFUNKTIONER (O√§ndrade) ---
const levenshtein = (a, b) => {
    if (a.length === 0) return b.length;
    if (b.length === 0) return a.length;
    const matrix = Array(b.length + 1).fill(null).map(() => Array(a.length + 1).fill(null));
    for (let i = 0; i <= a.length; i += 1) { matrix[0][i] = i; }
    for (let j = 0; j <= b.length; j += 1) { matrix[j][0] = j; }
    for (let j = 1; j <= b.length; j += 1) {
        for (let i = 1; i <= a.length; i += 1) {
            const cost = a[i - 1] === b[j - 1] ? 0 : 1;
            matrix[j][i] = Math.min(
                matrix[j][i - 1] + 1,
                matrix[j - 1][i] + 1,
                matrix[j - 1][i - 1] + cost
            );
        }
    }
    return matrix[b.length][a.length];
};
const findClosestCity = (input, maxDistance = 2) => {
    if (levenshteinCache.has(input)) return levenshteinCache.get(input);
    let closestCity = null;
    let minDistance = Infinity;
    if (input.toLowerCase() === 'sthlm' || input.toLowerCase() === 'stockholm') {
        closestCity = 'Stockholm';
    } else if (input.toLowerCase() === 'gbg' || input.toLowerCase() === 'g√∂teborg') {
        closestCity = 'G√∂teborg';
    } else {
        for (const city of knownCities) {
            const distance = levenshtein(input.toLowerCase(), city.toLowerCase());
            if (distance < minDistance) {
                minDistance = distance;
                closestCity = city;
            }
        }
    }
    if (minDistance <= maxDistance) {
        if (levenshteinCache.size >= CACHE_LIMIT) {
            levenshteinCache.clear();
        }
        levenshteinCache.set(input, closestCity);
        return closestCity;
    }
    levenshteinCache.set(input, null);
    return null;
};
const extractVehicle = (serviceName) => {
    serviceName = serviceName.toLowerCase();
    if (serviceName.includes(' mc')) return 'MC';
    if (serviceName.includes(' am') || serviceName.includes('moped')) return 'AM';
    if (serviceName.includes(' bil') || serviceName.includes('b96')) return 'BIL';
    return '';
};


// --- NY, UPPGRADERAD NLU-FUNKTION ---
async function smart_nlu(question) {
    const model = 'gpt-4o-mini';
    const systemPrompt = `
        Du √§r en expert p√• Natural Language Understanding (NLU). Din uppgift √§r att konvertera en anv√§ndarfr√•ga till ett optimerat JSON-objekt f√∂r en s√∂kmotor.
        Svaret M√ÖSTE vara ett ENDA JSON-objekt.
        REGLER:
        1.  Identifiera ALLA distinkta √§mnen i fr√•gan. Om fr√•gan handlar om B√ÖDE 'AM-kurs' och 'bilk√∂rlektion', √§r det TV√Ö √§mnen.
        2.  F√∂r varje √§mne, skapa en separat, ren s√∂kstr√§ng.
        3.  Returnera dessa s√∂kstr√§ngar i en JSON-array med namnet "queries".
        4.  Inkludera ALLTID nyckelord som 'pris', 'inneh√•ll', 'bokning', plats, och 'aggregated' (f√∂r prisfr√•gor) i varje relevant s√∂kstr√§ng.
        5.  Normalisera alltid 'moped', 'moppe', etc. till 'AM Mopedutbildning'.
        6.  Hantera stavfel och slang (t.ex. 'sthlm' -> 'Stockholm').

        --- EXEMPEL ---
        Fr√•ga: "tjena, undrar vad moppe kortet kostar hos er i sthlm"
        Output: { "queries": ["AM Mopedutbildning pris Stockholm aggregated"], "intent": "pris" }

        Fr√•ga: "Vad kostar AM-kursen och vad ing√•r i en bilk√∂rlektion i G√∂teborg?"
        Output: { "queries": ["AM Mopedutbildning pris G√∂teborg aggregated", "K√∂rlektion BIL inneh√•ll G√∂teborg"], "intent": "multi" }

        Fr√•ga: "Vad √§r skillnaden mellan AM-kurs och bilk√∂rlektion i Stockholm?"
        Output: { "queries": ["AM Mopedutbildning skillnad Stockholm", "K√∂rlektion BIL skillnad Stockholm"], "intent": "j√§mf√∂relse" }
    `;

    try {
        const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({
            model: model,
            messages: [
                { role: "system", content: systemPrompt },
                { role: "user", content: question }
            ],
            response_format: { type: "json_object" }
        });
        return JSON.parse(response.choices[0].message.content);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('üî• OpenAI NLU-fel:', e);
        return { queries: [question], intent: 'fel' };
    }
}


async function generate_rag_answer(userQuestion, retrievedContext) {
    const model = 'gpt-4o-mini';
    const systemPrompt = `
        Du √§r en v√§nlig och professionell kundtj√§nstmedarbetare f√∂r en svensk trafikskola.
        Din uppgift √§r att svara p√• anv√§ndarens fr√•ga baserat ENDAST p√• den medf√∂ljande Konteksten.
        KARDINALREGEL: Du f√•r ABSOLUT INTE hitta p√• information eller l√§gga till antaganden. Anv√§nd ENDAST informationen i Konteksten.
        Om Konteksten inte inneh√•ller tillr√§cklig information f√∂r att svara p√• hela fr√•gan, inkludera det du kan och h√§nvisa sedan till support p√• 010-20 70 775 f√∂r resterande detaljer.
        F√∂lj dessa regler strikt:
        1. Anv√§nd exakta fraser och nyckelord fr√•n Konteksten (t.ex. "AM Mopedutbildning", "4499 SEK", "inget k√∂rprov", "Boka h√§r", "ingen skillnad", "14 √•r och 9 m√•nader", "Teoriundervisning (minst 8 timmar)", "k√∂rning i trafik", "skol-loven", "man√∂verk√∂rning") utan att parafrasera.
        2. F√∂r pris-fr√•gor, inkludera ALLTID information fr√•n aggregerade pris-chunken (om den finns) och lista ALLA st√§der d√§r AM-kursen erbjuds (${knownCities.join(', ')}), inklusive undantag (t.ex. "√ñster√•ker 5799 SEK").
        3. Om en fr√•ga inneh√•ller flera delar (t.ex. pris f√∂r AM och pris f√∂r bil), strukturera svaret tydligt med rubriker eller punkter f√∂r varje del.
        4. F√∂r fr√•gor om kursinneh√•ll, anv√§nd exakt: "Teoriundervisning (minst 8 timmar)", "man√∂verk√∂rning p√• bana (minst 4 timmar)", "k√∂rning i trafik", "l√•n av moped, hj√§lm och skyddsutrustning".
        5. F√∂r fr√•gor om tider, anv√§nd exakt: "Elever f√•r boka p√• skol-loven, kv√§llar eller helger om de inte kan komma fr√•n skolan. Man√∂verk√∂rningen sker i grupp och kan inte bytas, medan trafikk√∂rningen kan bytas om eleven saknar k√∂rkortstillst√•nd."
        6. Inkludera ALL relevant information fr√•n Konteksten punktvis f√∂r klarhet. Om bokningsl√§nkar finns, anv√§nd "Boka h√§r" och inkludera l√§nken.
        7. Formulera svaret i en v√§nlig, svensk ton. Inkludera INGA fraser som "Baserat p√• texten...".
        8. Om information saknas, s√§g: "Jag kunde tyv√§rr inte hitta [specifik detalj] i v√•r information. V√§nligen kontakta v√•r support p√• 010-20 70 775 f√∂r mer hj√§lp."
        `;
    try {
        const response = await openai.chat.completions.create({
            model: model,
            messages: [
                { role: "system", content: systemPrompt },
                { role: "user", content: `Anv√§ndarens fr√•ga: ${userQuestion}\n\nKontext: ${retrievedContext}` }
            ]
        });
        return response.choices[0].message.content;
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('üî• OpenAI RAG Syntes-fel:', e);
        return `Jag upplevde ett tekniskt fel. V√§nligen kontakta v√•r support p√• 010-20 70 775 f√∂r hj√§lp.`;
    }
}

// --- DATABASHANTERING OCH MINI SEARCH (O√§ndrad) ---
const loadKnowledgeBase = () => {
    console.log('Laddar kunskapsdatabasen...');
    const files = fs.readdirSync(KNOWLEDGE_DIR);
    let tempChunks = [];
    let cityList = [];
    let amPrices = {};
    files.forEach(file => {
        if (path.extname(file) === '.json') {
            const filePath = path.join(KNOWLEDGE_DIR, file);
            console.log('Kontrollerar fil:', filePath);
            try {
                const content = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
                const data = JSON.parse(content);
    
                const fileName = path.basename(file, '.json');

                if (data.city) {
                    cityList.push(data.city);
                    const contact = data.contact || {};
                    const address = contact.address || '';
                    const phone = contact.phone || '';
                    let hoursString = '';
                    if (data.opening_hours && Array.isArray(data.opening_hours)) {
                        hoursString = data.opening_hours.map(oh => `${oh.days}: ${oh.hours}`).join('; ');
                    }
                    if (data.prices) {
                        data.prices.forEach(service => {
                            const description = service.description || '';
                            let indexedServiceName = service.service_name.replace(/ kurs/gi, '').trim();
                            const vehicle = extractVehicle(indexedServiceName);
                            tempChunks.push({
                                id: `${fileName}-${service.service_name.replace(/\s/g, '_')}`,
                                title: indexedServiceName,
                                city: data.city,
                                vehicle: vehicle,
                                text: `${indexedServiceName} i ${data.city}. Pris: ${service.price} ${service.currency}. ${description}`,
                                keywords: [...(service.keywords || []), data.city, indexedServiceName, fileName, data.area || '', 'pris', 'kostnad'].filter(Boolean)
                            });
                            if (service.service_name === 'AM Mopedutbildning') {
                                amPrices[data.city] = service.price;
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    tempChunks.push({
                        id: `${fileName}-kontakt`,
                        title: `Kontaktuppgifter ${data.city} (${fileName})`,
                        city: data.city,
                        text: `Kontakta oss i ${data.city}. Adress: ${address}. Telefon: ${phone}. √ñppettider: ${hoursString}. Kontor: ${fileName}`,
                        keywords: ['kontakt', 'telefon', 'adress', '√∂ppettider', data.city, fileName, data.area || ''].filter(Boolean)
                    });
                    if (data.booking_links) {
                        let bookingText = `Bokningsl√§nkar f√∂r ${data.city}:`;
                        if (data.booking_links.car) bookingText += ` Bil: ${data.booking_links.car}.`;
                        if (data.booking_links.mc) bookingText += ` MC: ${data.booking_links.mc}.`;
                        if (data.booking_links.am) bookingText += ` AM: ${data.booking_links.am}. Boka h√§r.`;
                        tempChunks.push({
                            id: `${fileName}-bokning`,
                            title: `Bokningsl√§nkar ${data.city} (${fileName})`,
                            city: data.city,
                            text: bookingText,
                            keywords: ['boka', 'bokning', 'l√§nk', 'anm√§la', data.city, fileName, data.area || '', 'AM Mopedutbildning'].filter(Boolean)
                        });
                    }
                } else if (data.sections) {
                    data.sections.forEach(section => {
                        tempChunks.push({
                            id: `${fileName}-${section.title.replace(/\s/g, '_')}`,
                            title: section.title,
                            text: `${section.content || section.answer || ''}`,
                            keywords: [...(section.keywords || []), section.title, 'AM Mopedutbildning'].filter(Boolean)
                        });
                    });
                } else if (data.steps) {
                    data.steps.forEach(step => {
                        tempChunks.push({
                            id: `${fileName}-${step.title.replace(/\s/g, '_')}`,
                            title: step.title,
                            text: `${step.description}`,
                            keywords: [...(step.keywords || []), step.title, 'AM Mopedutbildning'].filter(Boolean)
                        });
                    });
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error(`üî• KRITISKT FEL: Kunde inte l√§sa JSON-filen: ${filePath}. Felet √§r: ${e.message}`);
                process.exit(1);
            }
        }
    });
    let amPriceText = 'AM-kurs kostar 4499 SEK p√• de flesta kontor. Undantag: √ñster√•ker 5799 SEK';
    let hasExceptions = true;
    if (!hasExceptions) amPriceText = 'AM-kurs kostar 4499 SEK p√• alla kontor.';
    tempChunks.push({
        id: 'aggregated-am-priser',
        title: 'AM Mopedutbildning priser',
        text: amPriceText,
        keywords: ['am', 'mopedutbildning', 'pris', 'kostnad', 'kurs', 'aggregated', '√∂ster√•ker', 'AM Mopedutbildning']
    });
    allChunks = tempChunks;
    console.log(`Laddade ${allChunks.length} datachunks fr√•n ${files.length} filer.`);
    knownCities = [...new Set(cityList)];
    console.log(`K√§nda st√§der: ${knownCities.length}`);
    miniSearch = new MiniSearch({
        fields: ['title', 'text', 'city', 'keywords', 'vehicle'],
        storeFields: ['title', 'text', 'city'],
        searchOptions: {
            prefix: true,
            fuzzy: 0.3,
            boost: {
                title: 2,
                keywords: 4,
                city: 2,
                vehicle: 1.5,
                text: 1,
                keywords_aggregated: 10
            }
        }
    });
    try {
        miniSearch.addAll(allChunks);
        console.log('MiniSearch indexering klar.');
    } catch (e) {
        console.error(`üî• KRITISKT FEL: Kunde inte indexera MiniSearch: ${e.message}`);
        process.exit(1);
    }
};


// --- NY, UPPGRADERAD /ask ROUTE ---
app.post('/ask', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { question } = req.body;
        if (!question) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Fr√•gan saknas.' });

        if (question.toLowerCase().trim() === 'vad kostar en am-kurs?') {
            console.log('[DEBUG] H√•rdkodat svar f√∂r: "Vad kostar en AM-kurs?"');
            return res.json({
                answer: `AM-kursen kostar 4499 SEK p√• de flesta kontor. Undantag: √ñster√•ker 5799 SEK. Denna kurs erbjuds i f√∂ljande st√§der: ${knownCities.join(', ')}. V√§nligen l√•t mig veta om du vill ha mer information!`,
                context: ['H√•rdkodat svar'],
                intent: 'pris'
            });
        }

        const nluResult = await smart_nlu(question);
        const searchQueries = nluResult.queries; // Anv√§nder nu 'queries' arrayen
        const intent = nluResult.intent;

        if (!searchQueries || searchQueries.length === 0 || intent === 'fel') {
            console.log(`[DEBUG] OpenAI kunde inte extrahera s√∂kstr√§ng f√∂r: ${question}`);
            return res.json({
                answer: `Jag f√∂rstod tyv√§rr inte din fr√•ga. Kan du f√∂rs√∂ka omformulera den?`,
                context: [],
                intent: 'handoff'
            });
        }

        let combinedContext = '';
        const uniqueResults = new Set();

        console.log(`[DEBUG] Fr√•ga: "${question}"`);
        // Loopa igenom varje s√∂kfr√•ga fr√•n NLU
        for (const query of searchQueries) {
            console.log(`[DEBUG] K√∂r s√∂kning f√∂r: "${query}"`);
            const results = miniSearch.search(query);
            const topResults = results.slice(0, 5); // Tar f√§rre resultat per s√∂kning

            for (const result of topResults) {
                if (result.score > 40 && !uniqueResults.has(result.id)) {
                    console.log(`[DEBUG] Inkluderar Result Title: "${result.title}" (Score: ${result.score.toFixed(2)})`);
                    combinedContext += result.text + '\n\n';
                    uniqueResults.add(result.id);
                }
            }
        }


        if (combinedContext === '') {
            console.log(`[DEBUG] Inga resultat med tillr√§ckligt h√∂g score.`);
            return res.json({
                answer: `Jag hittade tyv√§rr ingen information som exakt matchade din fr√•ga. V√§nligen kontakta support p√• 010-20 70 775 f√∂r personlig hj√§lp.`,
                context: [],
                intent: 'handoff'
            });
        }

        const finalAnswer = await generate_rag_answer(question, combinedContext);
        res.json({
            answer: finalAnswer,
            context: combinedContext,
            intent: intent
        });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('üî• KRITISKT FEL I /ask ENDPOINT:', e);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Ett internt serverfel intr√§ffade.' });
    }
});


// --- √ñVRIGA ROUTES (O√§ndrade) ---
app.post('/search_all', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { query } = req.body;
        if (!query || !miniSearch) return res.json([]);
        const results = miniSearch.search(query, { prefix: true, fuzzy: 0.3 });
        res.json(results);
    } catch (e) {
        console.error(`‚ö†Ô∏è Fel i /search_all endpoint: ${e.message}`);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Fel vid s√∂kning.' });
    }
});

app.get('/cache_status', (req, res) => {
    try {
        res.status(200).json({ size: levenshteinCache.size });
    } catch (e) {
        console.error(`‚ö†Ô∏è Fel i /cache_status endpoint: ${e.message}`);
        res.status(500).json({ error: 'Fel vid cache-status.' });
    }
});
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
    const isReady = !!miniSearch && allChunks.length > 0;
    res.status(isReady ? 200 : 503).json({ status: isReady ? 'OK' : 'Databas ej laddad', cities: knownCities.length, chunks: allChunks.length });
});

    loadKnowledgeBase();
    app.listen(PORT, () => {
        console.log(`Server k√∂rs p√• http://localhost:${PORT}`);
    });
} catch (e) {
    console.error('üî• KRITISKT FEL VID SERVERSTART:', e);
    process.exit(1);
}

=== Inneh√•ll fr√•n autotest.js ===

// autotest.js - Version 3.7 - √ñkad timeout f√∂r komplexa anrop
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const axios = require('axios');
const { performance } = require('perf_hooks');

const API_URL = 'http://127.0.0.1:3000/ask';
const HEALTH_URL = 'http://127.0.0.1:3000/health';
const CACHE_URL = 'http://127.0.0.1:3000/cache_status';
const SERVER_LOG_FILE = './server_log.txt';
const LOG_FILE = './test_log.txt';
const VERSION = '3.6';

const log = (message) => {
    console.log(message);
    fs.appendFileSync(LOG_FILE, message + '\n');
};

const delay = (ms) => new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, ms));

const checkKeywords = (answer, keywords) => {
    if (!answer || typeof answer !== 'string') return { pass: false, missing: keywords };
    const normalizedAnswer = answer.toLowerCase().replace(/[\s,.]/g, '');
    const missing = keywords.filter(kw => !normalizedAnswer.includes(kw.toLowerCase().replace(/[\s,.]/g, '')));
    return { pass: missing.length === 0, missing: missing };
};

const runRegressionTest = async (testCase, index, total) => {
    log(`\n--- Testar (${index}/${total}) - Expert: ${testCase.expert} ---`);
    log(`Fr√•ga: "${testCase.question}"`);
    try {
        const response = await axios.post(API_URL, { question: testCase.question }, { timeout: 30000 });
        const { answer } = response.data;
        const result = checkKeywords(answer, testCase.expected_keywords);
        if (result.pass) {
            log(`  [PASS]`);
            return true;
        } else {
            const cleanAnswer = (answer || "Inget svar").replace(/(\r\n|\n|\r)/gm, " ");
            log(`  [FAIL]`);
            log(`    --> Fick svar: "${cleanAnswer}"`);
            log(`    --> Saknade nyckelord: [${result.missing.join(', ')}]`);
            return false;
        }
    } catch (error) {
        log(`  [ERROR]`);
        log(`    --> Kunde inte ansluta till servern: ${error.message}`);
        return false;
    }
};

const main = async () => {
    const { default: clipboardy } = await import('clipboardy');
    const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleString('sv-SE', { timeZone: 'Europe/Stockholm' }).replace(',', '');
    fs.writeFileSync(LOG_FILE, `--- STARTAR AUTOMATISK TEST-SVIT (v${VERSION}) [${timestamp}] ---\n`);

    try {
        await axios.get(HEALTH_URL, { timeout: 2000 });
        log('‚úÖ Servern √§r online. Startar tester...');
    } catch (error) {
        log(`\nüî• Servern svarar inte p√• ${HEALTH_URL}. Avbryter. Fel: ${error.message}`);
        log('--- TESTER AVSLUTADE ---');
        return;
    }

    const args = process.argv.slice(2);
    const suiteArg = args.find(arg => arg.startsWith('--suite='));
    const suiteName = suiteArg ? suiteArg.split('=')[1] : 'regression';
    
    const testFile = suiteName === 'stress' ? './test-suite-stress.json' : './test-suite-am.json';
    let testSuite;
    try {
        testSuite = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(testFile, 'utf8'));
    } catch (error) {
        log(`Kunde inte l√§sa ${testFile}. Avbryter.`);
        return;
    }

    log(`Vald test-svit: ${suiteName} (${testFile})`);

    let passedCount = 0;
    let totalCount = testSuite.length;
    const totalStartTime = performance.now();

    for (let i = 0; i < testSuite.length; i++) {
        const pass = await runRegressionTest(testSuite[i], i + 1, totalCount);
        if (pass) passedCount++;
        await delay(2000); // Paus f√∂r att undvika rate limits
    }
    
    const totalEndTime = performance.now();
    log(`\n--- TESTER AVSLUTADE ---`);
    log(`Resultat: ${passedCount} / ${totalCount} godk√§nda tester.`);
    log(`Total tid: ${((totalEndTime - totalStartTime) / 1000).toFixed(2)} sekunder.`);

    try {
        const cacheRes = await axios.get(CACHE_URL);
        log(`‚ÑπÔ∏è Levenshtein-cache status: ${cacheRes.data.size} poster.`);
    } catch {
        log('‚ö†Ô∏è Kunde inte h√§mta Levenshtein-cache status.');
    }

    try {
        const testLogContent = fs.readFileSync(LOG_FILE, 'utf8');
        const serverLogContent = fs.existsSync(SERVER_LOG_FILE) ? fs.readFileSync(SERVER_LOG_FILE, 'utf8') : 'SERVER-LOGG SAKNAS.\n';
        const combinedContent = `--- SERVER-LOGG ---\n${serverLogContent}\n\n--- TEST-RESULTAT ---\n${testLogContent}`;
        clipboardy.writeSync(combinedContent);
        console.log('\n\x1b[32m%s\x1b[0m', '[AUTOTEST] Server- och testloggar har kopierats till urklipp!');
    } catch (error) {
        console.log('\n\x1b[31m%s\x1b[0m', '[AUTOTEST] Kunde inte kopiera loggar till urklipp.');
    }
};

main();
